[30;1m108 | [0m[35m  possible overlaps between the read and the adapter.[0m

[30;1m110 | [0m[35m  stage because we want to be able to let the user provide a maximum[0m
[30;1m111 | [0m[35m  error rate (``-e``).[0m
[30;1m112 | [0m[35m  Also, using edit distance (that is, unit costs) allows using some[0m

[30;1m819 | [0m[35m  where the ``gzip`` program is available.[0m
